PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

# Example: image_search()

## Claim
Text: "Chinese officials in white protective hazmat suits carried people down a hallway to be quarantined for having COVID-19 in November 2022."

...

ACTIONS:
```
image_search("China officials white suits carry people")
image_search("China officials carry people COVID quarantine 2022")
```


Month-old girl pulled from rubble in Gaza after airstrike killed her parents
============================================================================

[World](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world)
 Mar 20, 2025 3:02 PM EDT

KHAN YOUNIS, Gaza Strip (AP) — As rescuers dug through the remains of a collapsed apartment building in Gaza’s Khan Younis on Thursday, they could hear the cries of a baby from underneath the rubble.

Suddenly, calls of “God is great” rang out. Health officials said most of the victims were women and children.

The strike that destroyed the infant girl’s home hit Abasan al-Kabira, a village just outside of Khan Younis near the border with Israel, killing at least 16 people, mostly women and children, according to the nearby European Hospital, which received the dead.

It was inside an area the Israeli military ordered evacuated earlier this week, encompassing most of eastern Gaza.

Nabil Abu Dagga, a relative of Ella’s family who lives nearby, rushed to the scene of the strike.

“People were sitting together and enjoying themselves on a Ramadan night, staying up together as a family,” he said. The baby girl stirred fitfully as paramedics checked her over.

Her parents and brother were dead in the overnight Israeli airstrike.

“When we asked people, they said she is a month old and she has been under the rubble, since dawn,” said Hazen Attar, a civil defense first responder. We never felt that there was stability, not at all.”

**READ MORE:** [Israeli strikes across Gaza hit multiple homes, killing at least 85 Palestinians](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/politics/israeli-strikes-across-gaza-hit-multiple-homes-killing-at-least-85-palestinians)

Israel resumed heavy strikes across Gaza on Tuesday, shattering the truce that had facilitated the release of more than two dozen hostages. The military did not immediately comment on the overnight strikes.

Hours later, the Israeli military restored a blockade on northern Gaza, including Gaza City, that it had maintained for most of the war, but which had been lifted under the ceasefire deal.

Hundreds of thousands of Palestinians had returned to what remains of their homes in the north after a ceasefire took hold in January.

The war began when Hamas-led militants stormed into southern Israel on Oct. 7, 2023, killing some 1,200 people and taking 251 hostage.

Israel’s blistering retaliatory air and ground offensive has killed nearly 49,000 Palestinians since then, more than half of them women and children, according to the Gaza Health Ministry. She had been born 25 days earlier, in the midst of a tenuous ceasefire that many Palestinians in Gaza had hoped would mark the end of a war that has devastated the enclave, killed tens of thousands and displaced nearly its entire population.

Only the girl’s grandparents survived the attack. Killed were her brother, mother and father, along with another family that included a father and his seven children. Rescuers digging through the rubble could be seen pulling out the small body of a child sprawled on the mattress where he had been sleeping.

The girl’s grandmother, Fatima Abu Dagga, sat with a group of other women in a relative’s house Thursday, taking turns cradling the infant. Her sons and their wives and eight grandchildren died in the bombing, and only the baby survived."

# Your Summary



===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
PBS News published an article on March 20, 2025, about an Israeli airstrike in Khan Younis, Gaza, that killed at least 16 people, mostly women and children. <image:6472> The article mentions a month-old girl was pulled from the rubble, while her parents and brother were killed. The article also mentions that the war began on October 7, 2023, and that nearly 49,000 Palestinians have been killed since then.

Gaza: Baby pulled alive from rubble after Israeli air strike on Rafah
=====================================================================

Rescuers in the city of Rafah, southern Gaza, have pulled a baby girl alive from the rubble after an Israeli air strike.

People used their hands to free Mariam Abu Akel from the debris, before a rescuer ran with her to a nearby hospital.

Doctors there swabbed her cuts.

The baby had been sheltering in a house with her family when the strike took place, which killed her mother and sister, Reuters reported. Her father and young brother survived.

The air strike killed 20 people and injured 55, according to a Hamas-run health ministry spokesperson.

More than 21,500 people - mostly children and women - have been killed during Israeli retaliatory attacks on Gaza, according to the Hamas-run health ministry. Thousands more are believed to be still under rubble of buildings destroyed by air and artillery strikes.

Israel launched its military campaign in Gaza after Hamas attacked southern Israel on 7 October, killing about 1,200 people - most of them civilians - and taking about 240 hostages.

29 December 2023

* If the Search Result doesn't contain any relevant information for the fact-checking work, simply print one word in capital letters: "NONE".

* Try to filter out relevant information even if the search result is in a different language.

# Record
## Claim
Claim: "<image:38> This image shows two children in Gaza in April 2025 found dead under the rubble of their home two months after an Israeli airstrike destroyed it."

## Actions
```
web_search("children found rubble home Gaza Israeli airstrike")
image_search("children found rubble home")
```

## Evidence
### Evidence from `web_search`
PBS News published an article on March 20, 2025, about an Israeli airstrike in Khan Younis, Gaza, that killed at least 16 people, mostly women and children, including a month-old girl whose parents and brother were killed (<image:6472>). The BBC published an article on December 29, 2023, about a baby girl pulled alive from the rubble after an Israeli air strike in Rafah, Gaza, which killed her mother and sister (<image:6474>, <image:6478>, <image:6480>, <image:6484>, <image:6486>, <image:6488>, <image:6492>). Democracy Now! reported on May 27, 2025, about an Israeli airstrike in Gaza that killed nine children, with emergency workers pulling charred bodies from the rubble (<image:6505>).


### Evidence from `image_search`
Al Jazeera published an article about children being pulled from the rubble in Turkey and Syria. ([https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/2/8/hope-heartbreak-as-children-pulled-from-rubble-in-turkey-syria](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2023/2/8/hope-heartbreak-as-children-pulled-from-rubble-in-turkey-syria)) <image:8752> The Guardian published a video of children being pulled from the rubble after their home was hit by an Israeli airstrike in Gaza. ([https://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2023/oct/19/gaza-moment-children-are-pulled-from-rubble-after-home-hit-by-israeli-airstrike-video](https://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2023/oct/19/gaza-moment-children-are-pulled-from-rubble-after-home-hit-by-israeli-airstrike-video)) <image:8753>

The UN News provides an image of a teddy bear in the rubble. ([https://news.un.org/en/story/2016/08/537042](https://news.un.org/en/story/2016/08/537042)) <image:8754>


# Your Analysis



===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
The evidence confirms that children have been found in the rubble of homes destroyed by Israeli airstrikes in Gaza. However, the evidence does not confirm the specific details of the claim, such as the exact date (April 2025) or the specific location. The image search results show that children have been pulled from the rubble in Gaza, but the evidence does not confirm the image's origin.

Therefore, the claim is not fully verifiable due to the lack of specific information about the image's origin and the exact circumstances.

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

The UN News provides an image of a teddy bear in the rubble. ([https://news.un.org/en/story/2016/08/537042](https://news.un.org/en/story/2016/08/537042)) <image:8754>


## Elaboration

However, the evidence does not confirm the specific details of the claim, such as the exact date (April 2025) or the specific location. Therefore, the claim is not fully verifiable due to the lack of specific information about the image's origin and the exact circumstances.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

# Search Result
From [Source](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/feb/25/israel-strikes-targets-in-southern-syria-after-demanding-demilitarisation): 
Content: "Photograph: Anadolu/Getty Images

This article is more than **5 months old**

Israel strikes targets in southern Syria after demanding demilitarisation
=========================================================================

This article is more than 5 months old

Military sites hit as Tel Aviv says it ‘will not allow southern Syria to become southern Lebanon’

Israeli warplanes have carried out several airstrikes on military targets outside Damascus and in southern Syria, as Israeli officials warned the country’s army not to move south of the capital city.

Israeli jets struck military sites late on Tuesday in the town of Kiswah, south of Damascus, as well as in the southern province of Deraa, local [Syrian media](https://www.syria.tv/%D8%B7%D8%A7%D8%A6%D8%B1%D8%A7%D8%AA-%D8%A5%D8%B3%D8%B1%D8%A7%D8%A6%D9%8A%D9%84%D9%8A%D8%A9-%D8%AA%D8%B3%D8%AA%D9%87%D8%AF%D9%81-%D8%AC%D9%86%D9%88%D8%A8%D9%8A-%D8%AF%D9%85%D8%B4%D9%82-%D9%88%D8%AA%D9%88%D8%BA%D9%84-%D8%A8%D8%B1%D9%8A-%D9%81%D9%8A-%D8%AF%D8%B1%D8%B9%D8%A7-%D9%88%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%82%D9%86%D9%8A%D8%B7%D8%B1%D8%A9)
 reported.

The Israeli defence minister, Israel Katz, confirmed the strikes in southern [Syria](https://www.theguardian.com/world/syria)
 and warned that Israel “will not allow southern Syria to become southern Lebanon”.

Katz added that “any attempt by the Syrian regime forces and the country’s terrorist organisations to establish themselves in the security zone in southern Syria will be met with fire”.

On Sunday the Israeli prime minister, Benjamin Netanyahu, demanded the complete demilitarisation of southern Syria.

Shortly after a Syrian rebel offensive led by Islamist opposition group Hayat Tahrir al-Sham [toppled the Assad regime on 8 December](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/dec/08/syrians-celebrate-fall-of-bashar-al-assad-after-five-decades-of-dynastic-rule)
, Israeli forces entered the UN buffer zone between Israel and Syria. Israeli forces have remained there ever since, despite protests by Syria’s new government and the UN, which monitors the demilitarised zone between the two countries.

[Israel’s air force also carried out hundreds of airstrikes](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2024/dec/10/israel-strikes-hundreds-of-military-targets-in-syria)
 against weapons depots, naval bases and Syrian military infrastructure in the weeks after the fall of the Assad regime in an attempt to prevent the weaponry from falling into rebel hands. Israeli airstrikes in Syria had mostly stopped since the new year.

Hours before the Israeli bombings on Tuesday, Syria condemned Israel’s invasion of the buffer zone and called for it to withdraw its forces from Syrian territory. However, Israel also views Syria’s new rulers with suspicion, with Israel’s foreign minister, Gideon Sa’ar, on Monday calling the new rulers of Syria a “jihadist, Islamist terror group”.

Syrian civil war")<br>    <br><br>U.S.-led intervention against ISIL<br><br>*   [US intervention](/wiki/US_intervention_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "US intervention in the Syrian civil war")<br>    *   [Timeline](/wiki/Timeline_of_US_intervention_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "Timeline of US intervention in the Syrian civil war")<br>        <br>    *   [List of operation](/wiki/2014_American_rescue_mission_in_Syria "2014 American rescue mission in Syria")<br>        <br>    *   [May 2015 raid](/wiki/May_2015_U.S._special_forces_raid_in_Syria "May 2015 U.S. Israel's government claimed this was to thwart any "potential threat" from post-war Syria.

Israel took advantage of the [power vacuum](/wiki/Power_vacuum "Power vacuum")
 created by the fall of former Syrian president [Bashar al-Assad](/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad "Bashar al-Assad")
 to increase the amount of territory it controlled by several hundred square miles.[\[100\]](#cite_note-105)
 Israel declared the [1974 Agreement on Disengagement](/wiki/Agreement_on_Disengagement_between_Israel_and_Syria "Agreement on Disengagement between Israel and Syria")
 with [Ba'athist Syria](/wiki/Ba%27athist_Syria "Ba'athist Syria")
 to be void.[\[101\]](#cite_note-cnn20241208a-106)
[\[102\]](#cite_note-107)
 Israel initially said this new invasion would be "temporary", but later said it would hold onto the territory for an "unlimited time".[\[103\]](#cite_note-108)
 Israel also launched extensive aerial and naval strikes on Syrian military targets across the country, under an operation codenamed **Operation Arrow of Bashan** ([Hebrew](/wiki/Hebrew_language "Hebrew language")
: מבצע חץ הבשן, [romanized](/wiki/Romanization_of_Hebrew "Romanization of Hebrew")
: _Mivtza Ḥetz HaBashan_).[\[104\]](#cite_note-109)
[\[105\]](#cite_note-110)
 Israel's campaign crippled Syria's military capabilities, including [its army](/wiki/Syrian_Army "Syrian Army")
 and [its navy](/wiki/Syrian_Navy "Syrian Navy")
, and destroyed its [chemical weapons](/wiki/Syrian_chemical_weapons_program "Syrian chemical weapons program")
 stockpiles.

Israel's campaign in Syria was internationally condemned and was accused of violating [international law](/wiki/International_law "International law")
.[\[106\]](#cite_note-ITWP-111)
 Syrian President [Ahmed al-Sharaa](/wiki/Ahmed_al-Sharaa "Ahmed al-Sharaa")
 condemned Israel's actions and demanded withdrawal, but also said his country was not in a position to be drawn into another war following the 14-year [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
.[\[107\]](#cite_note-112)
[\[108\]](#cite_note-aljazeera20241215-113)

On 25 February 2025, Israel deepened its invasion of southern Syria while conducting a wave of airstrikes there and in [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus")
, one day after demanding the [Syrian caretaker government](/wiki/Syrian_caretaker_government "Syrian caretaker government")
 demilitarize southern Syria. The IDF said that it suffered no casualties.[\[21\]](#cite_note-NewArab010225-22)
[\[152\]](#cite_note-158)

On 2 February, the IDF near [Jubata al-Khashab](/wiki/Jubata_al-Khashab "Jubata al-Khashab")
 and surrounding villages established [outposts](/wiki/Outpost_(military) "Outpost (military)")
 and [military bases](/wiki/Military_base "Military base")
 with calls for more [Israeli settlement](/wiki/Israeli_settlement "Israeli settlement")
 into the Golan Heights by Israeli officials.[\[153\]](#cite_note-159)

On 11 February, Israeli Army Radio reported that Israel would prolong the occupation of their newly invaded territory in Syria throughout 2025.[\[128\]](#cite_note-permanent-133)

On 23 February, the IDF confirmed that it had built at least nine army posts in Syria, including two on Mount Hermon and seven on the buffer zone.[\[154\]](#cite_note-160)

On 25 February, the IDF completed raids southern [Rif Dimashq](/wiki/Rif_Dimashq_Governorate "Rif Dimashq Governorate")
, in the villages of Al-Kiswa, and [Daraa](/wiki/Daraa "Daraa")
, in the vicinity of the city of [Izra](/wiki/Izra "Izra")
 and penetrating the outskirts of Al-Bakar village, and penetrated the administrative borders between the governorates of [Daraa](/wiki/Daraa_Governorate "Daraa Governorate")
 and [Quneitra](/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate "Quneitra Governorate")
 in southern Syria and the Ain al-Bayda area in the countryside of Quneitra in southern Syria, also taking the villages of Sidon Al-Golan and Sidon Al-Hanout in the countryside of Quneitra.[\[155\]](#cite_note-161)
[\[156\]](#cite_note-162)
 This came after plans to install advanced military technology, border fencing, and checkpoints in the borders of Gaza, Lebanon, and Syria.[\[157\]](#cite_note-163)

On 27 February, the [Islamic Resistance Front in Syria](/wiki/Islamic_Resistance_Front_in_Syria "Islamic Resistance Front in Syria")
 began forming military cells in Southern Syria, likely with Iranian backing.[\[158\]](#cite_note-164)

On 1 March, Netanyahu and Defense Minister Israel Katz ordered the IDF to prepare to defend the Druze community in [Jaramana](/wiki/Jaramana "Jaramana")
 following [clashes](/wiki/Druze%E2%80%93Syria_clashes_(2025%E2%80%93present) "Druze–Syria clashes (2025–present)")
 between Syrian security forces and a local group called the "[Jaramana Shield Brigade](/wiki/Jaramana_Shield_Brigade "Jaramana Shield Brigade")
" that left one Syrian soldier dead.[\[159\]](#cite_note-165)
[\[160\]](#cite_note-166)

On 8 March, the IDF announced that it carried out several raids in southern Syria the week prior, capturing and destroying weapons.[\[161\]](#cite_note-167)

On 19 March 2025, Israel launched its largest incursion yet, capturing the village of Al-Adnaniyah in the countryside of Quneitra Governorate.[\[162\]](#cite_note-168)

On 25 March, several Syrian gunmen attacked Israeli soldiers in [Kuwaya](/wiki/Kuwaya "Kuwaya")
. The possibility of Syria joining the [Abraham Accords](/wiki/Abraham_Accords "Abraham Accords")
 has been raised, although Israel has insisted on retaining its control over the [Golan Heights](/wiki/Golan_Heights "Golan Heights")
.[\[241\]](#cite_note-247)
 Syrian Foreign Minister [Asaad Al-Shaibani](/wiki/Asaad_al-Shaibani "Asaad al-Shaibani")
 stated that Syria aspires to return to the terms of the [1974 Disengagement agreement](/wiki/Agreement_on_Disengagement_between_Israel_and_Syria "Agreement on Disengagement between Israel and Syria")
.[\[242\]](#cite_note-248)
 Among the key obstacles is Syria's demand that Israel cease operating or striking targets within Syrian territory.[\[243\]](#cite_note-249)
 Israeli media have reported proposals involving Syria possibly regaining a third of the Golan Heights and annexing [Sunni](/wiki/Lebanese_Sunni_Muslims "Lebanese Sunni Muslims")
 regions in [North Lebanon](/wiki/North_Lebanon "North Lebanon")
 and the [Beqaa Valley](/wiki/Beqaa_Valley "Beqaa Valley")
, including the city of [Tripoli](/wiki/Tripoli,_Lebanon "Tripoli, Lebanon")
, in exchange for peace with Israel.[\[244\]](#cite_note-250)

Reactions
---------

### Involved parties

*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/40px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png)[Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel")
    : In December 2024, Israel's government said it was conducting a temporary military operation,[\[245\]](#cite_note-251)
     that the United States had been notified prior to going in, and that the State of Israel "does not interfere in the domestic conflict within Syria".[\[113\]](#cite_note-cnn20241208b-118)
     The IDF later said that they "may end up staying there for the foreseeable future".[\[246\]](#cite_note-c010-252)
     [Yair Lapid](/wiki/Yair_Lapid "Yair Lapid")
    , the [Leader of the Opposition](/wiki/Leader_of_the_Opposition_(Israel) "Leader of the Opposition (Israel)")
    , supported the operation but criticized Netanyahu's management, saying: "I would not have gone to the border to make provocative statements to the press and put us in conflict with the new Syrian government."[\[247\]](#cite_note-253)
     On 11 February 2025, Israeli Army Radio reported that the IDF's presence in Syria would be prolonged throughout 2025.[\[128\]](#cite_note-permanent-133)
     On 23 February 2025, Israeli Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu demanded the complete demilitarization of southern Syria in the provinces of [Quneitra](/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate "Quneitra Governorate")
    , [Daraa](/wiki/Daraa_Governorate "Daraa Governorate")
     and [Suweyda](/wiki/Suwayda_Governorate "Suwayda Governorate")
    , and the withdrawal of Syrian forces from Syrian territory south of Damascus.[\[248\]](#cite_note-254)
     Israeli Defense Minister [Israel Katz](/wiki/Israel_Katz "Israel Katz")
     said that Israeli forces would remain in southern Syria "for an indefinite period of time to protect our communities and thwart any threat."[\[249\]](#cite_note-255)
    
*   ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Flag_of_Syria_%282025-%29.svg/40px-Flag_of_Syria_%282025-%29.svg.png) [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria")
    : Syrian then-_de facto_ leader [Ahmed al-Sharaa](/wiki/Ahmed_al-Sharaa "Ahmed al-Sharaa")
    , who became president in 2025, declared that Syria remains committed to the 1974 agreement and does not seek conflict with Israel or any other country. |

| [Start of insurgency in Syria](/wiki/Early_insurgency_phase_of_the_Syrian_civil_war "Early insurgency phase of the Syrian civil war")<br> (Sept. His mother had sent him a letter two days earlier, urging him to halt Israel's airstrikes in Syria to enable the search for him to continue.[\[194\]](#cite_note-200)

On 29 December 11 people, mostly civilians, were killed in what is believed to be an Israeli airstrike on a former Syrian Army weapons depot in [Adra](/wiki/Adra,_Syria "Adra, Syria")
, near Damascus.[\[49\]](#cite_note-AdraStrike1-52)
[\[195\]](#cite_note-AdraStrike2-201)
[\[196\]](#cite_note-202)

#### 2025

On 15 January, the [Israeli Air Force](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force")
 struck a [Hay'at Tahrir al-Sham](/wiki/Hay%27at_Tahrir_al-Sham "Hay'at Tahrir al-Sham")
 vehicle convoy in [Quneitra Governorate](/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate "Quneitra Governorate")
, killing two HTS personnel and the mayor of a local village. SOHR reported "violent explosions" in southern Syria, especially Quneitra and Daraa.[\[224\]](#cite_note-230)
 On 8 June, IAF bombed a vehicle in southern Syria claiming to have killed a Hamas member, two others were injured as well.[\[225\]](#cite_note-231)

[![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Hay%27at_al-Arkan_21July_2025.jpg/250px-Hay%27at_al-Arkan_21July_2025.jpg)](/wiki/File:Hay%27at_al-Arkan_21July_2025.jpg)

Damage in the Syrian General Staff complex in Damascus following the Israeli airstrikes on 16 July 2025

On 16 July, [the IDF bombed the entrance](/wiki/July_2025_Damascus_airstrikes "July 2025 Damascus airstrikes")
 to the [Syrian military headquarters](/wiki/Hay%27at_al-Arkan "Hay'at al-Arkan")
 in Damascus as a warning, citing security concerns over the Syrian army's deployment to Suwayda to restore order amid the [July 2025 southern Syrian clashes](/wiki/Southern_Syria_clashes_(July_2025%E2%80%93present) "Southern Syria clashes (July 2025–present)")
.[\[226\]](#cite_note-232)
 Heavier strikes targeted the Syrian military headquarters complex and caused vast damage and destruction to the main building, later strikes targeted the vicinity of the [Presidential Palace in Damascus](/wiki/Presidential_Palace,_Damascus "Presidential Palace, Damascus")
.[\[227\]](#cite_note-233)
[\[228\]](#cite_note-Aj16Jul-234)
 The Syrian [Ministry of Health](/wiki/Ministry_of_Health_(Syria) "Ministry of Health (Syria)")
 reported at least three killed and 34 injured as a result of the attacks.[\[229\]](#cite_note-235)
 Airstrikes were also conducted by Israel on the same day on multiple targets across the [Suwayda](/wiki/Suwayda_Governorate "Suwayda Governorate")
 and [Daraa](/wiki/Daraa_Governorate "Daraa Governorate")
 governorates, including the [al-Tha'lah Military Airbase](/wiki/Al-Tha%27lah_Military_Airbase "Al-Tha'lah Military Airbase")
 and other military targets.[\[230\]](#cite_note-236)
[\[231\]](#cite_note-237)
[\[232\]](#cite_note-238)

On 26 August, Israeli drone strikes in the Damascus suburb of [Al-Kiswah](/wiki/Al-Kiswah "Al-Kiswah")
 killed eight Syrian soldiers, who SANA reported had uncovered surveillance equipment while on patrol. He also stated that Syria will not allow its territory to be used to attack other countries, including Israel.[\[250\]](#cite_note-256)
     Syria's UN ambassador, [Qusay al-Dahhak](/wiki/Qusay_al-Dahhak "Qusay al-Dahhak")
    , called on the UN Security Council to compel Israel to immediately cease its attacks and withdraw to the [Purple Line (ceasefire line)](/wiki/Purple_Line_(ceasefire_line) "Purple Line (ceasefire line)")
    .[\[251\]](#cite_note-257)
     Al-Sharaa criticized Israel's actions, saying they cannot be justified, but also emphasized that Syria is not in a position to be drawn into a new conflict.[\[108\]](#cite_note-aljazeera20241215-113)
    

### International

*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Flag_of_the_Arab_League.svg/40px-Flag_of_the_Arab_League.svg.png)[Arab League](/wiki/Arab_League "Arab League")
    : The Arab League condemned "attempts to expand occupation in the Golan Heights or to unilaterally nullify the 1974 disengagement agreement, actions that flagrantly violate international law."[\[252\]](#cite_note-l645-258)
    
*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/40px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png)[Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt")
    : Egypt condemned Israel for "exploiting Syria's current instability to expand its occupation and impose a new fait accompli, a clear violation of international law."[\[253\]](#cite_note-n780-259)
    
*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/40px-Flag_of_France.svg.png)[France](/wiki/France "France")
    : The [Foreign ministry](/wiki/Ministry_for_Europe_and_Foreign_Affairs_(France) "Ministry for Europe and Foreign Affairs (France)")
     asked Israel "to withdraw from the zone and to respect Syria's sovereignty and territorial integrity", describing the military deployment as a violation of the 1974 agreement.[\[254\]](#cite_note-260)
    
*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Flag_of_Iran.svg/40px-Flag_of_Iran.svg.png)[Iran](/wiki/Iran "Iran")
    : The [Foreign Ministry](/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Iran) "Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Iran)")
     spokesman said that "This aggression is a flagrant violation of the [United Nations Charter](/wiki/Charter_of_the_United_Nations "Charter of the United Nations")
    ," and "We demand an immediate response from the UN Security Council to stop the aggression and hold the occupation regime accountable."[\[255\]](#cite_note-m221-261)
    [\[256\]](#cite_note-o689-262)
    
*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Iraq.svg/40px-Flag_of_Iraq.svg.png)[Iraq](/wiki/Iraq "Iraq")
    : The [Foreign ministry](/wiki/Iraqi_foreign_ministry "Iraqi foreign ministry")
     issued a statement condemning the Israeli attacks on Syria as an "action \[that\] is a blatant violation of international law and relevant international resolutions" and called on the [UN Security Council](/wiki/UN_Security_Council "UN Security Council")
     to "fulfill its responsibilities by condemning this blatant aggression and taking necessary measures to end these violations."[\[257\]](#cite_note-263)
    
*    ![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_Jordan.svg/40px-Flag_of_Jordan.svg.png)[Jordan](/wiki/Jordan "Jordan")

     [Ayman Safadi](/wiki/Ayman_Safadi "Ayman Safadi")
     condemned the move, stating that "it violates [international law](/wiki/International_law "International law")
    ".[\[258\]](#cite_note-264)

     condemned Israeli attacks on Syria.[\[259\]](#cite_note-265)

     asserted that the move was a serious violation of international law and a dangerous development in an already volatile region. [Archived](http://web.archive.org/web/20250201130607/https://www.newarab.com/news/israeli-forces-come-under-fire-syria-first-invasion)
     from the original on 1 February 2025."

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

CNN  — 

The beachside home of Israeli leader Benjamin Netanyahu was damaged in a drone strike claimed by Hezbollah, video footage geolocated by CNN shows, in an attack that penetrated deep inside Israel even as the militant group reels from sustained Israeli bombardment.

Netanyahu and his wife were not at home at the time of Saturday’s attack in the coastal city of Caesarea and no-one was injured, according to Israeli officials.

But the incident has raised questions about how the drone evaded Israel’s air defenses even after Hezbollah’s leadership has been decimated and as Israel’s military ramps up strikes across swathes of Lebanon.

CNN affiliate Kan 11 published an exterior photo of the house showing damage to a window with cracks and what appears to be burn marks. The IDF said two drones were fired and that while one was intercepted, the other was not – due to what it said was a human error.

The attack on Netanyahu’s house comes at a time of a widening regional conflagration in the Middle East. Israel still has not carried out its expected response to Iran for a ballistic missile attack earlier this month and is continuing its military campaign against Hezbollah in Lebanon.

The incident also comes as the US is investigating a leak of highly classified US intelligence about Israel’s plans for retaliation against Iran following an October 1 Iranian missile barrage targeting Israel.

_CNN’s Eyad Kourdi and Ivana Kottasová contributed reporting._

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

PlanPrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

# Search Result
From [Source](https://cedmohub.eu/posts-share-doctored-prisoner-abuse-poll-from-israeli-tv-channel/): 
Content: "The false posts emerged after the news channel broadcast footage that appeared to show Israeli soldiers sexually abusing Palestinian prisoners at a military base.** 

“Israel’s Channel 12 asked a question in an Israeli public opinion poll: Do you agree with the claim that a soldier is allowed to rape a prisoner with his hands tied? <image:8979>

Screenshot of the false post, taken August 22, 2024

The posts emerged online after the United States [urged](https://www.barrons.com/news/us-urges-israel-to-probe-video-of-prison-sex-abuse-6316ea67)
 Israel to investigate and implement accountability following the circulation of a video that appeared to show soldiers sexually abusing a Palestinian prisoner on August 7 ([archived link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240822070528/https://www.barrons.com/news/us-urges-israel-to-probe-video-of-prison-sex-abuse-6316ea67)
).

The leaked surveillance video, broadcast on Channel 12, showed Israel soldiers hiding behind shields in what online commentators suggested was sexual acts performed on a prisoner the Sde Teiman base.

The Israeli military said it has opened an [investigation](https://www.barrons.com/news/israel-army-opens-probe-into-suspected-abuse-of-detainee-cf341d85)
 into “suspected abuse” of a detainee at the facility, known to be holding Palestinians arrested from Gaza during the war ([archived link](https://perma.cc/JAJ6-FJ6U)
).

Channel 12 hosted a [controversial debate](https://www.the7eye.org.il/526413)
 on August 7 in which panellists discussed whether the rape and abuse of Palestinian prisoners should be legalised ([archived link](https://perma.cc/A49R-S47W)
).

The war was triggered by Hamas’s unprecedented October 7 attack on Israel, which resulted in the deaths of 1,205 people, mostly civilians, according to an [AFP tally](https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240903-israel-pm-unbowed-by-pressure-as-gaza-war-rages-on)
 based on Israeli official figures ([archived link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240904021154/https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240903-israel-pm-unbowed-by-pressure-as-gaza-war-rages-on)
).

Israel’s retaliatory military campaign to destroy Hamas has killed 40,819 people, according to the health ministry in the Hamas-run territory.

The altered image was shared on Facebook by users based in [Malaysia](https://web.archive.org/web/20240822013834/https://www.facebook.com/plugins/post.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fzinnirahmuthalif%2Fposts%2Fpfbid023SwxWmk3NXhVA2xDdnruaXAqhSAH7y6FNtfppVPESkD7YZbhuyLyJ2n5nEcHWexNl&show_text=true&width=500)
 and [Singapore](https://web.archive.org/web/20240822014040/https://www.facebook.com/plugins/post.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fyanies14%2Fposts%2Fpfbid0MfEF2xoJ9w8YDfzj6JoTMzRmioadtsVRFNyU1F98tgA9MpsxZDA8YErHMRBd3tukl&show_text=true&width=500)
.

Similar false posts were also shared on social media platform X in [Pakistan](https://perma.cc/4PCV-CGAV)
 and the [United Kingdom](https://perma.cc/52PV-SRBE)
.

**Altered screenshot**

A reverse image search on Google found the [original footage](https://www.mako.co.il/news-channel12?subChannelId=b91e54300a2ef710VgnVCM200000650a10acRCRD&vcmid=622e1dba8a601810VgnVCM200000650a10acRCRD)
 of the news bulletin segment published by Channel 12 on its website on May 27, 2022 ([archived link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240822070753/https://www.mako.co.il/news-channel12?subChannelId=b91e54300a2ef710VgnVCM200000650a10acRCRD&vcmid=622e1dba8a601810VgnVCM200000650a10acRCRD)
).

The two-minute, six-second video shows an anchor presenting the news alongside the survey results that read in Hebrew: “Do you agree with the claim that the government relies on supporters of terrorism?”

The video’s Hebrew-language title translates to English as: “A year for the government: a survey of mandates”.

The timestamp for the clip screenshot used in the misleading post can be seen at the one-minute 46-second mark.

In the manipulated image, a blue box covered the screen, hiding the original question that was displayed with the results on a screen behind the news anchor.

Channel 12 subsequently apologised for the poll, Israeli newspaper Haaretz [reported](https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/2023-10-02/ty-article/.premium/leading-israeli-news-channel-apologizes-for-terror-supporters-poll/0000018a-f13e-dfa2-a99e-f97fd6ea0000)

).

65% of Israeli Jews oppose criminal prosecution for soldiers suspected of raping Palestinian detainees
======================================================================================================

A shocking new poll shows that almost two out of three Jewish Israelis oppose criminal prosecution for soldiers suspected of gang-raping Palestinian detainees at the Sde Teiman torture facility.

By [Jonathan Ofir](https://mondoweiss.net/author/jonathan-ofir/ "Posts by Jonathan Ofir")

[](https://www.addtoany.com/add_to/print?linkurl=https%3A%2F%2Fmondoweiss.net%2F2024%2F08%2F65-of-israeli-jews-oppose-criminal-prosecution-for-soldiers-suspected-of-raping-palestinian-detainees%2F&linkname=65%25%20of%20Israeli%20Jews%20oppose%20criminal%20prosecution%20for%20soldiers%20suspected%20of%20raping%20Palestinian%20detainees "Print")

A shocking [poll](https://www.inss.org.il/he/publication/august-2024/)
 published on August 18 by the Israeli Institute for National Security Studies surveys attitudes concerning various aspects of what Israel calls “Swords of Iron” — the genocide of the last ten months and counting. 

The poll asks, among else, how people would want to handle the soldiers suspected of [gang-raping Palestinian detainees at the Sde Teiman torture facility](https://mondoweiss.net/2024/08/israeli-medias-coverage-of-the-rape-of-palestinian-detainees-shows-support-for-sexual-violence-in-service-of-genocide/)
 if it turned out that the suspicions were strong. Two-thirds of Jewish Israelis are saying that there is simply nothing criminal here — only “bad behavior,” at worst. 

And this seems to strengthen the pattern that has been documented: not only do Israelis seem to generally enjoy watching [snuff videos](https://mondoweiss.net/2024/03/we-are-the-masters-of-the-house-israeli-channels-air-snuff-videos-featuring-systematic-torture-of-palestinians/)
 of this systemic torture — they generally support the sexual violence, including rape, that has accompanied it. There, they only offer a data tracker on six points, but it doesn’t include the Hebrew survey with its 23 points. 

So this is yet another unbelievable data point — gang rape as a weapon of war is not considered criminal by two out of three Jewish Israelis when it’s Israeli soldiers doing it to Palestinians (in the much-publicized gang rape case, the victim happens to be a civil servant, a policeman for the drug control department in Jabalia). 

When it comes to Palestinians, the blanket suspicion of affiliation with Hamas generates a rationale for revenge by which Palestinians are assumed to be involved with sexual violence, and when we speak about “disciplinary measures” here, it is not just systemic torture and sexual violence, it also reaches the level of murder through torture. In addition to wishing a “regulated policy” of rape existed in Israeli prisons, Shlezinger also advocated that the “terrorists” be “executed according to law.” And he shared that belief during his _apology_ for his rape advocacy.

It is a whole other world of impunity for Israeli soldiers. 65%, almost two out of three Jewish Israelis, opposed criminal prosecution, and would prefer them be “handled in a disciplinary manner, by the commanding level only.”

The survey asked the question:

> “Recently, the military prosecution requested to extend the arrest of the five soldiers suspected of gross abuse, and clarified that there is added evidence which strengthens the suspicion against them. The story has been updated._

[Palestinians](/topic/Palestinians)
[Disinformation](/topic/Disinformation)
[Noura Erakat](/topic/Noura%20Erakat)
[Channel 12](/topic/Channel%2012)

WASHINGTON (TND) — Rep. Erakat's now-deleted X post contained a doctored image of a poll seemingly conducted by Israel's Channel 12, according to [screenshots](https://x.com/yashar/status/1821337704711516313 "https://x.com/yashar/status/1821337704711516313")
 shared by users. "THAT is the disgrace, Alex."  

When reached for comment, Erakat reiterated to TND that it is "not a leap or a stretch" to believe such a poll would have been published by Channel 12. She noted the image circulated shortly after video was released of an alleged gang rape of a Palestinian prisoner by Israeli soldiers at detention facilitySde Teiman.

State Department spokesperson Matthew Miller on Wednesday called for an investigation related to the video, emphasizing claims of sexual abuse atSde Teiman are "horrific." Israel's Supreme Court has repeatedly convened to consider closingthe facility.

Erakat told TND it is "devastating" for Palestinian-Americans to see such footage, adding both a lack of media coverage and the outrage she and Rep. <image:8989>](https://cbsaustin.com/game-center#/games/guessword)

'Squad' member shares fake poll claiming most Israelis support rape of Palestinians
===================================================================================

* * *

by KRISTINA WATROBSKI | The National Desk

Fri, August 9th 2024 at 3:45 PM

Updated Fri, August 9th 2024 at 5:36 PM

![UserWay icon for accessibility widget](/resources/defaults/news_3.0/icons/accessibility/userway-transparent.svg)

![FILE - Rep. Tlaib drew backlash for sharing the post, including from Forward columnist Alex Zeldin, who [called](https://x.com/JewishWonk/status/1821335110844575919 "https://x.com/JewishWonk/status/1821335110844575919")
 the congresswoman "a disgrace."

"Why is Rashida Tlaib, a Member of Congress, openly distributing fake polls claiming an American ally is pro-rape?" Zeldin wrote on X. Ritchie Torres, D-N.Y., also [condemned](https://x.com/RitchieTorres/status/1821941043035594962 "https://x.com/RitchieTorres/status/1821941043035594962")
 the doctored image, calling "disinformation" a "new enemy of Israel on the social media age."

> A fake poll falsely accusing Israelis of endorsing rape against Palestinians is dangerous disinformation designed to delegitimize and demonize both the Jewish People and the Jewish State," the congressman said. Tlaib trusted me & posting this \[without\] cross checking was my mistake."  

"But surely u understand how one would take this poll to be true in light of video of gang rape of a Palestinian detainee & Knesset + public debate on whether such rape should be ok," she added. Rashida Tlaib, D-Mich., is drawing backlash for sharing a social media post which falsely claimed most Israeli citizens believe soldiers can sexually assault Palestinians.

Noura Erakat, a prominent Palestinian-American activist and Rutgers University professor, initially made the post Wednesday."

# Your Summary



===== > RESPONSE:  < =====
The search result from CBS Austin states that the image in the claim is a doctored version of a 2022 Channel 12 poll. The original poll asked respondents about the Israeli government's relationship with "terrorist supporters." The article mentions that Rep. Rashida Tlaib shared the doctored image. The article was published on August 9th, 2024. <image:8989>

JudgePrompt - QUERY:

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

# Instructions

* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

Carrier USS Abraham Lincoln Heads to Middle East as Iran Threatens Strikes Against Israel
=========================================================================================

[Sam LaGrone](https://news.usni.org/author/slagrone)

August 2, 2024 7:31 PM

! <image:8999>

USS Abraham Lincoln (CVN-72) departs Naval Station North Island on July 11, 2024. US Navy Photo

West Coast carrier USS _Abraham Lincoln_ (CVN-72) is setting sail to the Middle East from the Pacific to relieve the carrier USS _Theodore Roosevelt_ (CVN-71) and its strike group. guided-missile destroyers that intercepted cruise and ballistic missiles in the first combat use of the Standard Missile 3.

As of Monday, _Lincoln_ was operating in the vicinity of Hawaii following [its July 11 deployment](https://news.usni.org/2024/07/12/carrier-uss-abraham-lincoln-leaves-on-deployment-uss-theodore-roosevelt-now-in-the-middle-east)
 from San Diego and _TR_ was operating in the Persian Gulf, according to [USNI News Fleet and Marine Tracker](https://news.usni.org/2024/07/29/usni-news-fleet-and-marine-tracker-july-29-2024)
.

It’s unclear on the timing of the transition between the two strike groups. Eisenhower_ (CVN-69) and its escorts from being extended a third time, [USNI News first reported](https://news.usni.org/2024/06/21/uss-dwight-d-eisenhower-leaving-red-sea-pacific-carrier-heading-to-the-middle-east)
. The next East Coast carrier set to head to the region, USS _Harry S. Truman_ (CVN-75), is still off the East Coast and in the midst of its pre-deployment training, USNI News understands.

In addition, the three-ship Wasp Amphibious Ready Group with the embarked 24th Marine Expeditionary Unit is currently in the Eastern Mediterranean. The ARG, composed of USS _Wasp_ (LHD-1), USS _New York_ (LPD-21) and USS _Oak Hill_ (LSD-51), and the 24th MEU are in position in the event of a non-combatant evacuation of people from Lebanon, several defense officials have told USNI News.

The Pentagon also announced the deployment of unspecified fighter squadrons headed to the region.

“The Secretary of Defense has reiterated that the United States will protect our personnel and interests in the region, including our ironclad commitment to the defense of Israel,” reads the statement from the Pentagon.

## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `not enough information`: The fact-check does not contain sufficient information to come to an conclusion. For example,there is substantial lack of evidence or the evidence is inconclusive, conflicting or self-contradictory. In the case of a lack of evidence, state which information exactly is missing. In particular, if no RESULTS or sources are available, pick this decision.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.

# Instructions
The available knowledge is insufficient to assess the Claim. Therefore, **propose a set of actions** to retrieve new and helpful evidence. Adhere to the following rules:
* The actions available are listed under Valid Actions, including a short description for each action. No other actions are possible at this moment. 
* For each action, use the formatting as specified in Valid Actions.
* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `geolocate`
   * Description: Performs geolocation to determine the country where an image was taken.
   * How to use: Provide an image and the model will determine the most likely countries where it was taken.
   * Format: geolocate(<image:k>), where `k` is the image's ID

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

* Include all actions in a single Markdown code block at the end of your answer.
* Propose as few actions as possible, but as much as needed. Do not propose similar or previously used actions.



## Valid Actions
* `image_search`
   * Description: Run an image search on Google to retrieve related images for a given query.
   * How to use: This is a helpful tool for fact-checking images. Use this to retrieve images associated with a specific keyword or phrase. Ensure that the query is clear and specific to improve search accuracy. If no relevant images are found, refine the query or use more descriptive terms.
   * Format: image_search("your image search query goes here")

* `web_search`
   * Description: Run an open web search on Google or DuckDuckGO to retrieve any related webpage.
   * How to use: Do not use this with a previously used or similar query from previous web searches. If a previous web search did not yield any results, use a very different query.
   * Format: web_search("your web search query goes here")

# Example: image_search()

## Claim
Text: "Chinese officials in white protective hazmat suits carried people down a hallway to be quarantined for having COVID-19 in November 2022."

...

ACTIONS:
```
image_search("China officials white suits carry people")
image_search("China officials carry people COVID quarantine 2022")
```

# Example: web_search()

## Claim
Text: "New Zealand’s new Food Bill bans gardening"
Claim date: October 29, 2020

...

## Actions
```
web_search("New Zealand Food Bill 2020")
web_search("New Zealand Food Bill gardening ban")
```

## Claim

## Evidence
### Evidence from `web_search`
NPR reported on August 3, 2024, that the U.S. is sending more warships to the Middle East as Israel steps up attacks, with Israel expecting an attack from Iran and its allies ([https://www.npr.org/2024/08/03/nx-s1-5061738/the-u-s-is-sending-more-warships-to-the-middle-east-as-israel-steps-up-attacks](https://www.npr.org/2024/08/03/nx-s1-5061738/the-u-s-is-sending-more-warships-to-the-middle-east-as-israel-steps-up-attacks)). USNI News reported on August 2, 2024, that the USS Abraham Lincoln is heading to the Middle East in response to threats from Iran, and a three-ship Wasp Amphibious Ready Group is in the Eastern Mediterranean ([https://news.usni.org/2024/08/02/carrier-uss-abraham-lincoln-heads-to-middle-east-as-iran-threatens-strikes-against-israel](https://news.usni.org/2024/08/02/carrier-uss-abraham-lincoln-heads-to-middle-east-as-iran-threatens-strikes-against-israel)).

Military.com reported on September 20, 2024, about the increased U.S. military presence in the Middle East, including warships in the eastern Mediterranean Sea ([https://www.military.com/daily-news/2024/09/20/us-warplanes-ships-and-troops-ready-middle-east-if-conflict-expands.html](https://www.military.com/daily-news/2024/09/20/us-warplanes-ships-and-troops-ready-middle-east-if-conflict-expands.html)). <image:8996>, <image:8999>, <image:9009>


### Evidence from `image_search`
The web search results discuss U.S. warships en route to Lebanon. One article from L'Orient-Le Jour discusses this topic ([https://today.lorientlejour.com/article/1422223/which-american-warships-are-en-route-to-lebanon.html](https://today.lorientlejour.com/article/1422223/which-american-warships-are-en-route-to-lebanon.html)) and another from the Associated Press ([https://apnews.com/article/navy-warships-lebanon-hezbollah-israel-feec28090bed129618eda05e25a59b09](https://apnews.com/article/navy-warships-lebanon-hezbollah-israel-feec28090bed129618eda05e25a59b09)).

Stratfor also has an article on the topic ([https://worldview.stratfor.com/article/lebanon-what-us-warships-coast-do-and-do-not-mean](https://worldview.stratfor.com/article/lebanon-what-us-warships-coast-do-and-do-not-mean)). The search results include images of warships (<image:9017>, <image:9018>, <image:9019>).


## Elaboration
The evidence confirms that U.S. warships were deployed to the Middle East, including the Eastern Mediterranean, in August 2024. The evidence also mentions that the U.S. military presence was increased in the region due to threats from Iran and its allies. However, the evidence does not explicitly state that the warships were en route to the Lebanon coast to support the Israel Defense Forces (IDF).

Therefore, the claim is partially supported by the evidence, as it confirms the presence of U.S. warships in the region during the specified timeframe. However, the specific purpose of the deployment, as stated in the claim, is not directly supported by the provided evidence.

To fully verify the claim, additional information is needed to confirm the warships' destination and their specific mission in relation to the IDF.

Do NOT include:
* advertisements
* any other information not related to the Record or the Claim

Additional rules:
* Do not add any additional information besides the information in the Search Result.
* If the Search Result doesn't contain any relevant information for the fact-checking work, simply print one word in capital letters: "NONE".
* Keep your writing style like in the Examples 1, 2 and 3 provided to you.
* Try to filter out relevant information even if the search result is in a different language.

Courts

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Global courts | *   [_South Africa v. official confirmed that the United States was resuming its transfers of 500 pound bombs to Israel.[\[43\]](#cite_note-43)

In August 2024, the Biden administration approved a $20 billion arms sale to Israel, including F-15 fighter jets and tank and mortar shells.[\[44\]](#cite_note-44)
 The United States approved a $165 million sale of military tank trailers, including replacement parts, tool kits, and logistics support.[\[45\]](#cite_note-45)

### Naval and air support

The United States has provided naval and aerial support to Israel on multiple occasions since October 2023. So if we're going to start using that word, fine, let's use it appropriately."[\[90\]](#cite_note-Forbes-90)
 While suing [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden")
 as the largest provider of military aid to Israel, the [Center for Constitutional Rights](/wiki/Center_for_Constitutional_Rights "Center for Constitutional Rights")
 (CCR) argued that "the United States has the means available to have a deterrent effect on Israeli officials now pursuing genocidal acts against the Palestinian people in Gaza."[\[92\]](#cite_note-92)
 In a declaration in the lawsuit, Genocide scholar [William Schabas](/wiki/William_Schabas "William Schabas")
 said that in his view there was a "serious risk of genocide" and that the US was "in breach of its obligation" under the [1948 Genocide Convention](/wiki/Genocide_Convention "Genocide Convention")
 and international law.[\[93\]](#cite_note-TIMEBiden-93)
[\[94\]](#cite_note-CNSBiden-94)
 [Rashida Tlaib](/wiki/Rashida_Tlaib "Rashida Tlaib")
, a Democratic representative of Michigan, accused Joe Biden of supporting the "genocide of the Palestinian people".[\[95\]](#cite_note-95)

Following the [veto](/wiki/List_of_vetoed_United_Nations_Security_Council_resolutions "List of vetoed United Nations Security Council resolutions")
 of another resolution in the UN Council on 8 December 2023, international human rights organizations issued the following statement: "By continuing to provide Israel with weapons \[and\] diplomatic cover as it commits atrocities, including collectively punishing the Palestinian civilian population in Gaza, the US risks complicity in war crimes."[\[96\]](#cite_note-Aljazeeradec9-96)

During an August 2024 meeting with humanitarian aid organizations, U.S. The survey also found a 53% sum total majority support for withdrawing military aid from Israel if it rejected the ceasefire proposal, including 70% of Democrats, 51% of Independents, 53% of swing voters, and 35% of Republicans, with 36% being against it.[\[205\]](#cite_note-205)
[\[206\]](#cite_note-206)

According to a [Chicago Council on Global Affairs](/wiki/Chicago_Council_on_Global_Affairs "Chicago Council on Global Affairs")
 poll released on 6 August 2024, and conducted online between 21 June and 1 July 55% of all sum total respondents oppose using US troops to defend Israel if it is attacked by a neighboring country, whereas 41% support it.[\[207\]](#cite_note-207)
[\[208\]](#cite_note-208)
[\[209\]](#cite_note-209)
 According to a Pew Research in 2025, more than half of American adults (53%) express an unfavorable opinion of Israel, compared to 42% in March 2022 - before 7 October 2023.[\[210\]](#cite_note-210)

### Israeli officials

Some Israeli government members believed that Biden's support for Israel was not strong enough. **[^](#cite_ref-483)
    ** [Over 800 Jewish scholars urge Biden to not sign IHRA antisemitism bill](https://www.newarab.com/news/800-jewish-scholars-urge-biden-reject-antisemitism-bill)
