Iran

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [2024 conflict](/wiki/2024_Iran%E2%80%93Israel_conflict "2024 Iran–Israel conflict") | *   [Israeli airstrike on the Iranian consulate in Damascus](/wiki/Israeli_airstrike_on_the_Iranian_consulate_in_Damascus "Israeli airstrike on the Iranian consulate in Damascus")<br>    <br>*   2024 Iranian strikes in Israel<br>    *   [April](/wiki/April_2024_Iranian_strikes_on_Israel "April 2024 Iranian strikes on Israel")<br>        <br>    *   [October](/wiki/October_2024_Iranian_strikes_on_Israel "October 2024 Iranian strikes on Israel")<br>        <br>*   2024 Israeli strikes on Iran<br>    *   [April](/wiki/April_2024_Israeli_strikes_on_Iran "April 2024 Israeli strikes on Iran")<br>        <br>    *   [October](/wiki/October_2024_Israeli_strikes_on_Iran "October 2024 Israeli strikes on Iran")<br>        <br>*   [Assassination of Ismail Haniyeh](/wiki/Assassination_of_Ismail_Haniyeh "Assassination of Ismail Haniyeh") |
| [2025 war](/wiki/Iran%E2%80%93Israel_war "Iran–Israel war") | *   [Casualties](/wiki/Casualties_of_the_Iran%E2%80%93Israel_war "Casualties of the Iran–Israel war")<br>    <br>*   [Weizmann Institute of Science strikes](/wiki/Iranian_strikes_on_Weizmann_Institute_of_Science "Iranian strikes on Weizmann Institute of Science")<br>    <br>*   [Evin prison strikes](/wiki/Israeli_strikes_on_Evin_prison "Israeli strikes on Evin prison")<br>    <br>*   [U.S. foreign aid](/wiki/United_States_foreign_aid "United States foreign aid")
, 1946–2022[\[12\]](#cite_note-aid-12)

After Hamas gunmen attacked Israel on 7 October, resulting in the death of 1,139 Israelis, 695 of which were civilians, Israel began a campaign against Gaza.[\[13\]](#cite_note-Holland-13)
[\[14\]](#cite_note-14)
 Since the start of the Israeli operation, more than 39,000 Palestinians in Gaza have been killed, of whom 52% of identified were women and children.[\[15\]](#cite_note-15)
[\[16\]](#cite_note-16)
 Several thousand more are missing and presumed trapped under rubble.[\[17\]](#cite_note-17)
[\[18\]](#cite_note-18)
 Israel placed Gaza under a complete blockade, including the prevention of fuel and water from entering the Gaza Strip.[\[19\]](#cite_note-Harbaljazeera-19)
[\[20\]](#cite_note-20)
[\[21\]](#cite_note-21)
[\[22\]](#cite_note-Al_Jazeera-22)
[\[23\]](#cite_note-23)
 The United States described Hamas' preemptive attack as "unprovoked,"[\[24\]](#cite_note-Guardian-24)
 and started sending warships and warplanes into the region, prepared to give Israel whatever it needs.[\[25\]](#cite_note-TimeCOPP-25)
 Civil rights groups such as the [Center for Constitutional Rights](/wiki/Center_for_Constitutional_Rights "Center for Constitutional Rights")
 meanwhile called on the government to address the underlying issues that have led to the recent violence, such as Israel's 56-year illegal [possession of the Palestinian lands](/wiki/Israeli-occupied_territories "Israeli-occupied territories")
 and its [16-year blockade of Gaza](/wiki/Blockade_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Blockade of the Gaza Strip")
 as well as "the [apartheid regime](/wiki/Israel_and_apartheid "Israel and apartheid")
 throughout historic Palestine".[\[26\]](#cite_note-SperiTheintercept-26)

Between 1946 and 2024, it has received $228 billion in military aid from the United States, making it the greatest recipient in history.[\[27\]](#cite_note-27)
 Following Israel's victory over surrounding Arab forces in the [1967 Six-Day War](/wiki/Six-Day_War "Six-Day War")
 and its subsequent occupation of the West Bank, East Jerusalem, and Gaza, military assistance to the country surged significantly. fighter jets, along with the U.K., France, and Jordan, shot down [Iranian drones and missiles](/wiki/April_2024_Iranian_strikes_against_Israel "April 2024 Iranian strikes against Israel")
 directed at Israel.[\[46\]](#cite_note-46)
 In June 2024, the United States sent the [USS _Wasp_](/wiki/USS_Wasp_(LHD-1) "USS Wasp (LHD-1)")
 and its marines aboard to serve as a deterrent to Hezbollah in its conflict with Israel.[\[47\]](#cite_note-47)
 In August 2024, the United States deployed the [USS _Abraham Lincoln_ Carrier Strike Group](/wiki/Carrier_Strike_Group_3 "Carrier Strike Group 3")
, equipped with stealth [F-35C Lightning II](/wiki/Lockheed_Martin_F-35_Lightning_II "Lockheed Martin F-35 Lightning II")
 combat jets, and the ballistic missile submarine [USS _Georgia_](/wiki/USS_Georgia_(SSGN-729) "USS Georgia (SSGN-729)")
, to Israel.[\[48\]](#cite_note-48)

In October 2024, the United States deployed the [Terminal High-Altitude Area Defense](/wiki/Terminal_High-Altitude_Area_Defense "Terminal High-Altitude Area Defense")
, along with 100 U.S. He must halt the offensive arms sales to Israel that enable its relentless bombing of Gaza and Lebanon."[\[76\]](#cite_note-76)

In May 2025, a pro-Palestinian protest was held in [Denver](/wiki/Denver "Denver")

# Instructions
**Determine the Claim's veracity** by following these steps:
1. Briefly summarize the key insights from the fact-check (see Record) in at most one paragraph.
2. Write one paragraph about which one of the Decision Options applies best. Include the most appropriate decision option at the end and enclose it in backticks like `this`.




## Decision Options
* `true`: The claim is factually accurate when it is confirmed by evidence from multiple and reliable sources.
* `false`: The claim is not factually accurate. This is the case if one of the following three conditions is met:(1) The claim is demonstrably false when it is disproven by evidence from multiple and reliable sources,(2) The claim or image is taken out of context, i.e. the origin, content and/or meaning of a statement or an image is misrepresented. For example, an old claim or an old image is mispresented in a new context in a misleading way,(3) There is not enough evidence to verify the claim or the evidence is conflicting or self-contradictory.
